\bentry
\wordRemoveSpace{N,-n}{N, n}
\pron{enf}
\gl{\nA}(\bava\ \eng{Ns} yA \eng{N's}).
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} iMgilxSf vaNaRmAleya hadinAlakxneya akaSxra. 
\num{2} mudarxNadalilx agalada mAna (= \eng{\hyperref{kandict_e.pdf}{E}{en}{en}.}) 
\num{3} (\biVga) enf: \eng{N;} anidiRSaTx sithxra saMKeyx.
\num{4} (\Bwvi) avogADorx sithxra(da saMkeVta).}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{\eng{to the n$^{th}$ (\engit{or} nth) degree}
\alnum{a} yAvudAdarU beVkAda GAtakekx. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) eSaTxkekx beVkAdarU; paramAvadhige.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[nail(1)]{nail}
\pron{neVlf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} uguru; naKa.
\num{2} (maqgagaLa, hakikxgaLa kAlina) moneyuguru. 
\num{3} (maqdu kokikxna hakikxgaLa) kokikxna meVlABxgadalilxna uguru padAthaRda gaTiTxgaMti.
\num{4} moLe; ANi. 
\num{5} gajada \eng{1/16} BAga; \eng{$2\frac{1}{4}$} aMgula (hiMde
baLasutitxdadx baTeTxya oMdu aLate).}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng {bite one's nail} (aBAyxsabaladiMda yA tALemxgeTuTx) uguru kaDi.
\num{2} \eng {drive nail in one's
\hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{coffin(1)nuga}{${}^1$coffin}.}
\num{3} \eng{hard as nails}

\alnum{a} daqDhakAyanAgi; gaTiTxmuTATxgi.

\alnum{b} kalelxdeya; nidaRya; kaThiNa.
\hypertarget{nailpagu4}{}
\num{4} \eng{hit the nail on the head}

\alnum{a} sariyAda sapxSaTxne koDu.

\alnum{b} yAvudu sariyoV A kelasa mADu.

\alnum{c} gurimuTuTx.
\num{5} \eng{hit the right nail}= \hyperlink{nailpagu4}{\pagu\ \eng{(4).}}
\num{6} \eng{nail -- biting} tiVvarx AtaMkavanunxMTumADuva. 
\num{7} \eng{on the nail} (\kanmu\ haNa pAvatiya \vi) takaSxNa; kUDaleV; taDavilalxde.
\num{8} \eng{right as nails} sari; nija; Kare; KaMDita sari.
\num{9} \eng {tooth and nail} shakitxyanenxlAlx biTuTx; balavAgi paTuTx hiDidu: 
\eng{fight tooth and nail} balavAgi paTuTx hiDidu hoVrADu.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[nail(2)]{nail}
\pron{neVlf}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} moLehoDe; moLe hoDedu -- BadarxpaDisu, baMdhisu. 
\num{2} (vayxkitx, gamana, \mo vanunx) baMdhisu; calisadaMtiDu; nATisu:
\eng{surpise nailed him to the spot} AshacxyaRdiMda avanu nishacxlanAgi niMta.
\num{3} (manuSayx, vasutx, \mo vanunx) BadarxpaDisu; hiDi; nililxsiko.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{nail (a lie etc.) to counter}(suLuLx \mo vanunx) bahiraMgapaDisu; 
suLeLxMdu toVrisu; suLaLxnunx etitx toVrisu.
\num{2} \eng{nail \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{color(1) nuga(9)}{${}^1$colour}s to the mast.}
\num{3} \eng{nail down}

\alnum{a} sapxSaTxvAgi vivarisu.

\alnum{b} (obabx vayxkitxyanunx avanu) koTaTx vacana \mo vugaLige kaTiTxhAku, baMdhisu.

\alnum{c} kaTaTx kaDeyadAgi niSakxSeR mADibiDu.

\alnum{d} (oMdu vasutxvanunx) moLe hoDedu bigi mADu, BadarxpaDisu.
\num{4} \eng{nail up}

\alnum{a} (bAgilu \mo vanunx) moLegaLiMda mucucx.

\alnum{b} (vasutxvanunx) moLegaLa sahAyadiMda BadarxpaDisu, nililxsu, kaTuTx.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{naked}
\pron{neVkiDf}
\gl{\gu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} naganx; betatxleya; nivARNa; bTeTx toTiTxrada; barimeYyina; nivaRsanada:
\eng{as naked as my mother bore me} namamxmamx haDedAga heVgidedxnoV aMtha batatxle sithxtiyalilx.
\num{2} arakiSxta; sulaBavAgi guriyAda, sikikxda; rakaSxNe ilalxda: \eng{left naked to temptations}
sulaBavAgi parxloVBanegaLige sikikxda.
\num{3} oreyilalxda; kApilalxda: \eng{a naked sword} oreyiMdeLeda katitx.
\num{4} naganx; mucucxmareyilalxda; sapxSaTx; suPxTa; neVravAda:
\eng{naked truth} naganxsatayx.
\num{5} (pariVkeSxgAgi hodike) terediTaTx: \eng{his naked soul} avana terediTaTx Atamx.
\num{6} baTaTxbayalAda; maragiDagaLilalxda; baMjaru: \eng{naked
shores} baTaTx bayalAda karAvaLi.
\num{7} rahita; ilalxda.
\num{8} elegaLilalxda; boVLAda: \eng{naked trees} boVLu maragaLu.
\num{9} (baMDe \mo vugaLa \vi) naganx; mucucxkaLeda; tereda.
\num{10} (nelada \vi) maNuNx, giDagaMTegaLiMda mucicxrada.
\num{11} (koThaDiya \vi) piVThoVpakaraNagaLilalxda; KAli.
\num{12} alaMkAravilalxda; niralaMkaqta; nirABaraNavAda.
\num{13} (hacicxda moVMbatitx \mo vugaLa \vi) gALigoDiDxda; sulaBadAhayx
anilagaLigoDiDxda; mucacxde terediTaTx.
\num{14} boVLuboVLAda; sipepx, ele, kUdalu, shalakxgaLu, cipupx, \mo vugaLilalxda.
\num{15} bariya; keVvala; AdhArarahita: \eng{naked assertion} AdhArarahita heVLike.
\num{16} yAvudeV sAdhanada neravilalxda; bariya: \eng{naked eye} (dUradashaRka, sUkaSxmXdashaRka, \mo vugaLa
neravilalxde noVDuva) bariya kaNuNx.}

\bentry
\word[narrow(1)]{narrow}
\pron{nAYxroV}
\gl{\gu}(\tara\ \eng{narrower,} \tama\ \eng{narrowest}).
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} kaDameyagalada; agala kaDameyAda; (udadxkekx takakxMte) Agala sAlada.
\num{2} (\vAyx) (savxrada \vi) nAlage kirunAlagegaLanunx bigumADi ucacxrisuva; saMkucita; saMvaqta.
\num{3} kiridAda; ikakxTATxda; kiSikxMdada: \eng{within narrow bounds} kiridAda
parimitiyoLage.
\num{4} saMkucita; parimita: \eng{in the narrowest sense} tiVrA saMkucita athaRdalilx.
\num{5} kaDimeyAgiruva; alapx parxmANada; savxlapx aMtarada: \eng{a
narrow majority} atayxlapx aMtarada bahumata.
\num{6} daqSiTxveYshAlayxvilalxda.
\num{7} anukaMpavilalxda.
\num{8} audAyaRvilalxda; saNaNx manasisxna; anudAra.
\num{9} durAgarxhada.
\num{10} parxteyxVkateya.
\num{11} sAvxthaRda; savxvicAra maganx.

\hyperdef{N}{natural(2)7}{}
\num{7} (isipxVTATadalilx)

\alnum{a} pAMTUnf \eng{(pontoon)} eMba isipxVTATadalilx ele haMcidAga
modalu \eng{21} aMka gaLisuva ATagAra.

\alnum{b} (kArxyXpfsx ATadalilx dALagaLiMda) ELu yA hanonxMdara -- gara
uruLisuvudu, hAkuvudu, eseyuvudu. 
\num{8} maMkAda nasu haLadi mishirxta kaMdu(baNaNx).}

\bentry
\word{naturalism}
\pron{nAYxcaralisa\kern -1ptZmf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} sahaja kirxye; sAvxBAvika kirxye; sahaja
 parxvaqtitxgaLiMda parxcoVditavAda kirxye; sahaja parxvaqtitxgaLiMda
 parxcoVditavAda kirxye, kAyaR.
\hypertarget{naturalism(2)}{}
\num{2} pArxkaqtika dhamaR; neYsagiRka dhamaR; sahaja dhamaR; keVvala
parxkaqtiyanunx, nisagaRvanunx Adharisiruva niVti shAsatxrX yA
matadhamaR.
\num{3} (\tashA) parxkaqti vAda; nisagaR vAda; savxBAva vAda; BwtavAda;

\alnum{a} jagatitxna saqSiTxge matutx sithxtige yAvudeV nisagARtiVta
yA AdhAyxtimxka kAraNa matutx shakitx beVkAgilalx, adu savxtaMtarx
savxyaMBu savxyaMpUNaR matutx savxyaM niyaMtarxka, adu
EkameVvAdivxtiVya satayx, mAnava adara oMdu aMga -- eMba sidAdhxMta;
jagatatxnunx kuritaMte yAvudeV atimAnuSa yA AdhAyxtimxka
parigaNaneyanunx nirAkarisuva daqSiTx, vAda; keVvala neYsagiRka
kAraNagaLu matutx niyamagaLu jagatitxnalilx elalxvanUnx
vivarisabalalxveMba vAda. 

\alnum{b} elalx neYtika niNaRyagaLU vasutxniSaThx vaNaRnegaLu matutx
avanunx pArxyoVgikavAgi pariVkiSxsabahudu eMba vAda.

\alnum{c} (\deVva) matadhamaRda elalx tatatxvXgaLU nisagaRda kirxyegaLa
adhayxyanadiMdaleV anugatavAgutatxve, avakekx deVva parxkAshana
beVkAgilalx eMba vAda. 
\num{4} (sAhitayx, kale) yathAthaR citarxNa; yathAthaRvAda; vAsatxvikate; vAsatxvika badukanunx AdashiRVkarisade, adu iruvaMteyeV pUNaR vivaragaLoMdige vasutxniSaThxvAgi, neYtika niNaRyagaLa soVMkilalxde, yathAvatAtxgi citirxsuva, vaNiRsuva vidhAna yA adanunx kurita sidAdhxMta.
\num{5} sahaja vataRne; sAvxBAvika parxvaqtitx; saMparxdAyagaLa bagegx
alakaSxyX, upeVkeSx.}

\bentry
\word{nature}
\pron{neVcarf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} (asitxtavxkekx AvashayxkavAda) vasutxvina sahaja --
 guNa, savxrUpa, lakaSxNa, dhamaR. 
\num{2} (aneVka veVLe \eng{Nature)}(manuSayxna, pArxNiya)
parxkaqti; savxBAva: \eng{it is not in her nature to act like that} A
riVti naDeyuvudu avaLa savxBAvavalalx. 
\num{3} manuSayx jAtiya savxBAva, lakaSxNa matutx BAvanegaLu.
\num{4} manuSayx savxBAvada vishiSaTx aMsha: \eng{the rational nature}
veYcArika savxBAva.
\eng{animal nature} pashu (pArxyavAda) savxBAva. \eng{moral nature} neYtika savxBAva.
\num{5} vishiSaTx savxBAvavuLaLx vayxkitx: \eng{sanguine natures do
 not feel this}... AshAvAdi savxBAvadavarige, AshAvAdigaLige idara
arivu iruvudilalx.
\num{6} tera; bage; riVti; vagaR: \eng{things of this nature of a
request} idu koVrikeya riVtiyadu.
\num{7} (manuSayxna shiVlavanunx, kirxyeyanunx nidhaRrisuva AMtarika)
parxvaqtitxgaLu; perxVraNegaLu. 
\num{8} parxkaqti; nisagaR; jaDajagatitxna GaTanegaLige kAraNavAda Bwtashakitx.
\num{9} parxkaqti vAyxpAra; (samaSiTxyAgi) nisagaRkirxye(gaLu).
\num{10} parxkaqti (deVvi); mUtiVRkaqta nisagaR (shakitxgaLu):
\eng{all nature looks gay} parxkaqtiyelalxvU naliyutitxde. \eng{Nature is the best physician} parxkaqti atuyxtatxma veYdayx.
\num{11} sasayx, pArxNi, BUdaqshayx, \mo\ nisagaRda aMshagaLu:
\eng{nature gives him comfort} nisagaR avanige nemamxdi koDutatxde.
\num{12} kaqSi mADada yA kADu parxdeVsha.
\num{13} asaMsakx qta sithxti, samAja, \mo vu.
\num{14} (\kanmu\ kaNiNxge AkaSaRkavAda) gArxmINa, gArxmAMtara -- parxdeVsha; haLiLxgADu.
\num{15} (vayxkitxtavxnunx parxBAvisuva yA nidhaRrisuva aMshavAgi) AnuvaMshiVyate \eng{(nurture}ge virudadhxvAgi).
\num{16} jiVviyoMdara jeYvika caTuvaTike yA jiVvanAvashayxkategaLu:
\eng{such a diet does not support nature} aMtha AhAra jiVvapoVSaNege sAladu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{against nature} savxBAvavirudadhxvAda; asAvxBAvika; aneYtika.
\num{2} \eng{against (\engit{or} contrary to) nature}

\alnum{a} pavADa sadaqsha.

\alnum{b} pavADasadaqshavAgi.

\alnum{c} \eng{back to nature} maraLi parxkaqtige; sahaja pArxkaqta
enanxbahudAda jiVvanasithxtige hiMdiruguvike.
\num{4} \eng{by nature} savxBAvataH
\num{5} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_e.pdf}{E}{ease(2) nuga(1)}{${}^2$ease} nature.}
\num{6} \eng{from nature} (kale \mo vugaLa \vi) parxkaqtiya, nisagaRda
vasutxgaLanunx mAdariyAgi baLasikoLuLxvudu: \eng{paint from nature}
parxkaqtiyanunx anusarisi citirxsu.
\num{7} \eng{human nature} mAnava savxBAva; manuSayxra sAmAnayx lakaSxNa, BAvagaLu, \mo vu.
\hyperdef{N}{nature pagu(8)}{}
\num{8} \eng{in a state of nature}

\alnum{a} pArxkaqta sithxti \eng{(state of grace} eMbudakekx virudadhxvAda padagucacx).

\alnum{b} (samAjavu vayxvasethxgoLuvudakikxMta pUvaRda) manuSayxna
anAgarika sithxti, asaMsakx qta sithxti.

\alnum{c} (pArxNigaLa, sasayxgaLa \vi) paLagisilalxda, rUDhisilalxda -- sithxti.

\alnum{d} batatxleya sithxti.
\num{9} \eng{in nature}

\alnum{a} vAsatxvavAgi (asitxtavxdalilx) iruva.

\alnum{b} elilx beVkAdarU; EnAdarU; yAvudeV riVtiyalilx.
\hypertarget{naturepagu10}{}
\num{10} \eng{in (\engit{or} by \engit{or} from) the very nature of
 the case} tatavxshaH; vasutxtaH.
\num{11} \eng{in (\engit{or} by \engit{or} from) the very nature of
 things}= \hyperlink{naturepagu10}{\pagu $(10)$}.
\num{12} \eng{in \engit{or} of the nature of} A vagaRdaMtha yA
A vagaRkekx seVrida: \eng{in the nature of an excuse} nepada riVtiya.
\num{13} \eng{in the \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{course(1) pagu(5)}{${}^1$course} of nature}.
\num{14} \eng{law of nature = \hyperlink{natural law}{natural law}.}
\num{15} \eng{one of Nature's} oMdu vagaR yA samudAyada atayxMta
sahaja parxtinidhiyAda: \eng{one of Nature's gentlemen} sahaja
sajajxna; huTuTx saBayx; parxkaqtiyalilx janamxtALida obabx sahaja
sajajxna vayxkitx.}

\word[nay(1)]{nay}
\pron{neV}
\gl{\kirxvi}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} (\pArxparx) =\eng{\hyperlink{no(4)}{${}^4$no}.}
\num{2} (matotxbabxna heVLikege asamamxti sUcisuvalilx) (\pArxparx)
Eke? oLeLxyadu!
\num{3} alalxde; matutx; adakikxMta hecAcxgi:
\eng{weighty, nay, unanswerable} tUkavAdadudx, aSeTxV alalx, parxti heVLalAgadaMthadu.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[nay(2)]{nay}
\pron{neV}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} `ilalx', eMba shabadx; (nakArAtamxka utatxra
 heVLuvalilx) `ilalx', `Agadu',
`kUDadu', eMba shabadx itAyxdi: \eng{will not take nay} ``Agadu"
enunxvudanunx avanu 
opupxvudilalx, sivxVkarisuvudilalx.
\num{2} virudadhx mata, OTu: \eng{counted 16 nays} hadinAru virudadhx
matagaLanunx eNisida.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
{\eng{say nay} `Agadu', `ilalx' inunxvudu; `uhuM' eMdu heVLuvudu: 
\eng{cannot say him nay} avanige Agadu enanxlAgadu.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[near(1)]{near}
\pron{niarf}
\gl{\kirxvi}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} (sathxLadalAlxgali, kAladalAlxgali) samiVpadalilx;
 samiVpavAgi;
hatitxravAgi; hatitxradalilx: \eng{the station is quite near} nilAdxNa bahaLa samiVpadalilxde.
\num{2} (\pArxparx) bahumaTiTxge; inunx savxlapxdaralilx: \eng{he was
 as near as could be to 
being knocked down by a bus} savxlapxdaralilx basusx avana meVle haridu hoVguvudaralilxtutx.
\num{3} hatitxra hatitxra: \eng{as near as one can guess, there were
forty people} hatitxra
hatitxra alilx nalavatutx janaridadxru.
\num{4} (\pArxparx) bahaLa lekAkxcAravAgi; jipuNatanadiMda: \eng{he lives very near}
avanu bahaLa jipuNatanadiMda jiVvana naDesutAtxne.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{far and near} elalx kaDe; elelxlUlx.
\num{2} \eng{go near to do (\engit{or} come \engit{or} go near doing) (something)}
inenxVnu mADuvudaralilxru.
\num{3} \eng{near at hand}

\alnum{a} sulaBavAgi keYge sikukxvaMte; hatitxradalelxV: \eng{always have a
dictionary near at hand} yAvAgalu shabadxkoVshavanunx hatitxraveV iTuTxkoMDiru.

\alnum{b} (kAlada \vi) hatitxradalelxV; bahaLa dUravAgirade; anatikAladalelxV:
\eng{the examinations are near at hand} pariVkeSxgaLu hatitxravAgalive.
\num{4} \eng{near by} hatitxradalelxV; anati dUradalelxV.
\num{5} \eng{near upon} (\pArxparx) iSaTxralelxV; anatikAladalelxV: \eng{it was near upon
2 o'clock} inenxVnu eraDu gaMTeyAguvudaralilxtutx.
\num{6} \eng{nowhere near} hatitxraveVnU Agirade; aSeTxVnU hatitxravalalxde; dUradalilx
(Aguva saMBavavilalx eMbathaRdalilx): \eng{the cinema was nowhere near
full} calanacitarx
maMdira aSeTxVnU BatiRyAgiralilalx.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[near(2)]{near}
\pron{niarf}
\gl{\upa}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} (deVsha, kAla, sithxti yA hoVlikeyalilx, yAvudoV oMdara yA oMdakekx) hatitxra;
anatidUra; samiVpa: \eng{the sun is near setting} sUyaR muLuguvudaralilxdAdxne. \eng{the time
draws near Christmas} kirxsfmasf(kAla) hatitxra barutitxde.
\num{2} (samAsa padagaLalilx):

\alnum{a} hoVluva; sadaqsha; badali; parxtiyAda: \eng{near beer} biyarfnaMthadu.

\alnum{b} hecucxkaDame; mukAkxlu mUru viVse pAlu; bahuteVka: \eng{near-hysterical}
 hecucx kaDame unAmxda sithxtiyalilx. \eng{a near-Communist}
hecucxkaDame kamUyxnisfTx.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{comes no nearer to the end} kone muTuTxvaMteyeV ilalx.
\num{2} \eng{near the \hyperref{kandict_k.pdf}{K}{knuckle(1) nuga(2)}{${}^1$knuckle}.}
\num{3} \eng{(sail) near the wind}

\alnum{a} (gALiya otatxDada neraviniMda) eSuTx sAdhayxvoV aSuTx edurugALige edurAgi yAna mADu.

\alnum{b} (\AmA) ashilxVlatege yA apArxmANikatege hatitxravAgi.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[near(3)]{near}
\pron{niarf}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} hatitxrada; nikaTa saMbaMdhada: \eng{near
relation} hatitxrada saMbaMdhi.
\num{2} Apatx; anoyxVnayx: \eng{a near friend} Apatx senxVhita.
\num{3} eDagaDeya (\eng{off} padakekx vayxtirikatxvAgi): \eng{the near
foreleg} eDagaDeya muMgAlu.
\num{4} (sAthxna yA kAla) hatitxraviruva; samiVpada; nereya; pakakxda.
\num{5} (rasetx yA hAdi) neVravAda.
\num{6} bahu hatitxrada: \eng{a near guess} bhuteVka sariyAda Uhe. \eng{a near resemblance}
 hatitxrada hoVlike.
\num{7} alapx aMtarada: \eng{near escape} alapx aMtaradalilx Ada pAru.
\num{8} jugagx; jipuNatanada: \eng{he is very near with his money} avanu tananx haNada
viSayadalilx bahaLa jugagx.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{near and dear} namamxvaru tamamxvaru; iSaTxbaMdhugaLu:
naMTariSaTxru; ApetxVSaTxru.
\num{2} \eng{near miss} (\rUpa\ saha)

\alnum{a} (bAMbu \mo vugaLa \vi) gurige hatitxravAda; savxlapxdaralilx guri tapipxda.

\alnum{b} savxlapxdaralilx GaSaRNe, Dikikx tapipxda parisithxti.

\alnum{c} (parxyatanxda \vi) hecucxkaDime yashasivxyAda, Adare pUtiR udedxVsha sAdhisirada.
\num{3} \eng{near thing} savxlapx aMtaradalilx Ada pAru.}

 mugisalu nAnu sharxmapaDuvudilalx.

\alnum{a} kutitxgege baru; pArxNApAyada, kaThiNavAda -- peTuTxtinunx, anuBavisu.

\num{7} \eng{neck or nothing} AdadAdxgaleMdu gelalxlu idudxdelalxvanUnx paNavoDuDx.

huTiTxsuva, taruva vasutx \mo vu.

yA hucucxhucAcxgi mAtanADu.

\eng{debt is negative capital} sAlavu niSeVdharUpada baMDavALa.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}

\bentry

\pron{neTf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} (huri, hagagx, kUdalu, \mo vugaLiMda mADida) bale;
 jAla; kalilx. 
\num{2} (mIVnu \mo vanunx hiDiyuvudakekx baLasuva) bale.
\num{3} (mucucxva, aDakavAgisuva, rakaSxNeya, tuMbi hiDidukoMDu
hoVguva, \mo\ upayoVgagaLuLaLx) bale.
\num{4} (PuTfbAlf \mo\ ATagaLalilx goVlf parxdeVshavanunx mucacxlu, Tenisf \mo\ ATagaLalilx ATada parxdeVshavanunx viBAgisalu hAkuva) bale.
\num{5} (neYtika yA mAnasikavAgi) inonxbabxnanunx, oMdanunx hiDidu hAkuva sAdhana; bale.
\num{6} (obabx vayxkitxyanunx moVsadiMda hiDiyalu baLasuva) baleyaMtha karxma yA sAdhana.
\num{7} jeVDana bale.
\num{8} jAlabaMdha; heNeda baleya kelasa.
\num{9} (\bava dalilx) (balegaLiMda) sututxvareda kirxkeTfna aBAyxsa meYdAna.

\num{2}eMdeMdigU ilalx; yAvatUtx AgalAradu: \eng{it is never likely
 to succeed} adu eMdigU yashasivxyAgalAradu.
\num{3} beVDa; bAradu: \eng{never fear} hedarabeVDa.
\num{4} (\AmA) (AshacxyaR yA saMdeVsha sUcisuvalilx) Ce, elAlxdarU uMTe! eMdigU ilalx!

mIVri hoVgadu; tididxkoLuLxvudAdare eMdAdarU tididxkoLaLxbahudu.
\num{3} \eng{never is a long day} = \hyperlink{never pagu4}{\pagu $(4)$}.
\hypertarget{never pagu4}{}
\num{4} \eng{never is a long time}(duDukina tAyxga yA nirAse yA

sAdhayxvilalx' eMdu duDuki heVLabAradu.

\num{6} \eng {never a one} obabxnU ilalx; oMdU ilalx.
\num{7} \eng{never ending} eMdeMdigU mugiyada.
\num{8} \eng{never \hyperref{kandict_m.pdf}{M}{mind(2) pagu(6)}{${}^2$mind}.}
\num{9} \eng{never-never}(otitx heVLuvalilx) eMdigU ilalx; ilalxveV ilalx.

\num{11} \eng{never so}(hiMde) aSoTxMdu mitimiVri eMdU mADalilalx.

kelasa avana shakitx miVridAdxgitutx -- hiMdeMdU avanu aSuTx mitimiVri 
parxyAsapaTiTxralilalxvAdarU saha.

\bentry
\word{news}
\pron{nUyxsf\kern -1ptZ}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (\sA\ \Eva vAgi \parx) sudidx; vAteR; samAcAra; (hosa) vataRmAna;
vaqtAtxMta; hosa viSaya; hosa GaTane: \eng{have you heard this news}I sudidx keVLididxVyeVnu?
\num{2} sudidx parxsAra mAdhayxma.
\num{3} (kulxpatx, hosa) sudidx samAcAragaLa bAnuli parxsAra.
\num{4} \eng{News}(vaqtatxpatirxkegaLa hesarina BAgavAgi baruva) 
samAcAra patirxke, \udA\ \eng{Evening News}.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{bad news}

\alnum{a} keTaTx sudidx; ashuBa vAteR. 

\alnum{b} (\AmA) ahitakara vayxkitx yA vasutx.
\num{2} \eng{be news} (Iga tAneV keVLida) hosa viSaya: \eng{that is news to me}
A sudidx nAnu I tanaka keVLiyeV iralilalx.
\num{3} \eng{good news} shuBavAteR; oLeLxya sudidx.
\hyperdef{N}{news pagu(4)}{}
\num{4} \eng{no news is good news} sudidxyilalxdiruvudeV oMdu oLeLx
sudidx; sudidxyilalxdiruvudu oLeLxya sithxtiyanunx sUcisutatxde.
\num{5} \eng{that is no news} adu elalxrigU gotitxruva samAcAra; adeVnU hosa sudidxyalalx.
\num{6} \eng{be in the news} (sudidxyanunxMTumADuvaSuTx) parxsidadhxvAgu: 
\eng{she was in the news last year} hoVda vaSaR avaLadedxV sudidx.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[next(1)]{next}
\pron{nekfsfTx}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} pakakxda; nereya; samiVpada; atayxMta hatitxrada; magugxlalilxruva;
pakakxdalilx vAsisuva: \eng{my next neighbour} nananx pakakxda nereyavanu.
\num{2} oDaneyeV anusarisi baruva, hiMdeyeV baruva; mAraneya; AmeVlina; muMdina: 
\eng{will ask the next man} muMde sikukxvavananunx keVLutetxVne. 
\eng{next Friday} muMdina shukarxvAra.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{next but one} pakakxdadxriMdAceya;
pakakxda oMdanunx biTuTx Aceya.
\num{2} \eng{next \hyperref{kandict_d.pdf}{D}{door(1) nuga(10)}{${}^1$door} to.}
\num{3} \eng{next to}

\alnum{a} (\rUpa) hecucx kaDame; bhumaTiTxge; bhuteVka: \eng{next to impossible}
hecucx kaDame asAdhayx.

\alnum{b} (obabxna jate) bahaLa geLetanadiMda; saligeyiMda.
\num{4} \eng{the next man}(yAvaneV) sAmAnayx manuSayx; shirxV sAmAnayx.
\num{5} \eng{the next world} paraloVka.}
\eentry

\num{2} AmeVle; muMde; taruvAya; oMdara naMtara:

baMda.}}

\bentry
\word[next(4)]{next}
\pron{nekfsfTx}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} pakakxda, samiVpada -- vayxkitx, vasutx, \mo vu.
\num{2} AmeVle baMda, taruvAyada -- vayxkitx, vasutx, \mo vu:
\eng{she was the next to arrive} AmeVle baMdavaLu avaLu; avaLu AmeVle baMdaLu.
\num{3} muMdina kAgada, saMcike, \mo vu: \eng{will tell you in my next}
nananx muMdina kAgadadalilx heVLutetxVne.
\num{4} muMdina vAra \mo vu: 
\eng{the Friday after next} muMdina shukarxvArada anaMtarada shukarxvAra.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\hyperdef{N}{next(4) pagu(1)}{}
\num{1} \eng{next of kin}(badukiruvavaralilx) hatitxrada naMTaru; samiVpa baMdhugaLu.
\num{2} \eng{next please}

\alnum{a} idu sAku, muMdina parxshenx keVLi.

\alnum{b} nimamxdu Ayitu, muMdinavanu barali.}
\eentry

\bentry

\pron{neYsf}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} sogasina.
\num{2} sUkASx mxBiruciya.
\num{3} kusubiSeTxya; mecicxsalu kaSaTxvAda.
\num{4} nAjUkina.
\num{5} niyamaniSaThx.
\num{6} niSakx qSaTx; karAruvAkAkxda.
\num{7} kaTuTxniTATxda: \eng{must not be too nice about the means}
sAdhanoVpAyagaLa bagegx bahaLa kaTuTxniTATxgirabAradu.
\num{8} niSakx qSaTxte; gamana, EkAgarxte, ecacxrike, kwshala, viveVcanegaLu -- avashayxvAda:
\eng{a nice experiment} kwshaladiMda kUDida parxyoVga.
\num{9} sUkaSx mxvAda:
\eng{a nice shade of meaning} sUkaSx mxvAgi noVDabeVkAda athaRda CAye.
\num{10} ati sUkaSx mxviveVcaneya; sUkaSxmXgArxhiyAda:
\eng{a nice ear} sUkaSxmXgArxhiyAda kivi.
\num{11} (\AmA) 

\alnum{a} hitavAda; AkaSaRka; ramayx; manoVhara; koVmala.

\alnum{b} rucikara; suvAsanABarita.

\alnum{e} senxVhapara.

\alnum{h} (vayxMgayx) avalakaSxNavAda; keTaTxdAda; avayxvasethxya; asahayxkara:

\bentry
\word{night}
\pron{neYTf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} iruLu; rAtirx; nishe; sUyARsatxdiMda sUyoRVdayadavaregina kAla.
\num{2} iruLa katatxle: \eng{went forth into the night} katatxloLakekx hoVda.
\num{3} (\alaMshA) aMdhakAra sithxti; tamasusx; rAtirxya katatxlinaMtha sithxti.
\num{4} mucacxMje; mabubx; saMdhAyxkAla; muMgatatxle: \eng{shall not reach home before night}
mucacxMjeya oLage (katatxlu kaviyuva munanx) mane talupalAre.
\num{5} rAtirxya -- have, anuBavagaLu yA kelasa kAyaRgaLu.
\num{6} (nATaka \mo) parxdashaRnagaLu naDeyuva saMje: \eng{first
night} nATakada modalaneya
(rAtirx) parxdashaRna.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\hypertarget{night pagu1}{}
\num{1} \eng{all night} iruLelalx; rAtirxyiDiV.
\num{2} \eng{all night long} = \hyperlink{night pagu1}{\pagu $(1)$}.
\num{3} \eng{at night} saMjeyalilx; katatxlAda meVle; rAtirxyalilx; saMje \eng{6}riMda 
madhayxrAtirxyavaregina kAladalilx: \eng{ten o'clock at night}rAtirx hatutx gaMTe.
\num{4} \eng{black (\engit{or} dark) as night} rAtirxyaMtha kapupx; iruLugapupx; iruLinaMtha katatxlu.
\num{5} \eng{by night} rAtirxyalilx; iruLa mareyalilx.
\num{6} \eng{have a bad night} rAtirx niderxyilalxde bAdhepaDu.
\num{7} \eng{have a good night} rAtirx suKa niderx mADu.
\num{8} \eng{last night} hiMdina, kaLeduhoVda, atayxMta Icina -- rAtirx.
\num{9} \eng{make a night of it} rAtirxyelAlx utasxva samAraMBadalilx kaLe.
\num{10} \eng{night and day} hagaliruLU; eDebiDade; yAvAgalU; sadA.
\num{11} \eng{spend the night with} (\sA\ leYMgika saMbaMdhavanunx sUcisuva athaRdalilx) (\kanmu)
rAtirx malagalu avakAsha paDe.
\num{12} \eng{stay the night} rAtirx taMgu; (maneyiMdAce) beLagAguvavarege uLiduko.
\num{13} \eng{turn night into day} dinada hAge rAtirx iDiV
(agatayxvAda ujavxla diVpagaLa beLakinalilx) kelasa mADu. 
\num{14} \eng{work nights} rAtirxya saradiyalilxru.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[nine(1)]{nine}
\pron{neYnf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} oMbatutx.
\num{2} oMbatatxra saMkeVta: \eng{9; IX; ix.}
\num{3} oMbatatxneya saMKeyx; oMbatutx.
\num{4} (isipxVTele) oMbatutx; oMbatutx cihenxgaLiruva ele.
\num{5} oMbatutx gaMTe samaya.
\num{6} (aLate itAyxdi) oMbatatxneya saMKeyx.
\num{7} navaka; oMbatutx vasutx itAyxdigaLiruva taMDa, guMpu.
\num{8} (\bava dalilx) \eng{9}neya aLateya keYgavasu, pAdarakeSx, itAyxdi.
\num{9} (\ame) beVsfceMDATada taMDa, daLa.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{cat has nine lives} bekukx sulaBavAgi sAyuvudilalx.
\num{2} \eng{dressed up to the nines} atayxMta ThiVkAgi. pariSAkxravAgi-uDupu dharisida.
\hyperdef{N}{nine(1) pagu(3)}{}
\num{3} \eng{nine days' wonder} oMbatutx dinada AshacxyaR; savxlapxkAla bahu AkaSaRkavAgidudx beVga maretuhoVguvaMthadudx.
\num{4} \eng{nine tenths} hatatxralilx oMbatutx BAga; hecucx kaDame pUtiRyAgi.
\num{5} \eng{nine times out of ten} (\birx) sAmAnayxvAgi; bahuteVka; mukAkxlu mUru viVse pAlu.
\num{6} \eng{nine to five} oMbatatxriMda aidaravarege: sAmAnayxvAgi kaceVriya kelasada veVLe.
\num{7} \eng{possession is nine points of the law} oMdu vasutxvina sAvxdhiVnAnuBavavidadxre adara meVle hatatxralilx oMbatutx pAlu nAyxyAnukUlavAda hakukx idadxMteyeV.
\num{8} \eng{the Nines} oMbatutx kAvayx deVviyaru.
\num{9} (\birx\ \eng{999}) tutuR seVvege miVsalAda dUravANi saMKeyx.}

\bentry
\word{nipper}
\pron{niparf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} gALavanunx yA itara miVnugaLanunx kacucxva miVnu.
\num{2} (\birx) (\asaM) cikakx huDuga yA huDugi; poVra yA poVri.
\num{3} (\bava dalilx) cimuTa; cimuTa katatxri; balavAgi kacicx
hiDidukoLuLxvudakAkxgali taMti \mo vanunx katatxrisuvudakAkxgali
baLasuva, davaDeyaMtha BAgagaLuLaLx Ayudha. 
\num{4} (\bava dalilx) (\pArxparx) kacucxkananxDaka; mUgukananxDaka;
mUgige kacicxkoLuLxva kananxDaka.
\num{5} kudureya bAcihalulx.
\num{6} (EDi, naLiLx, \mo) valakxvaMtavagaRda pArxNigaLa cimuTAMga, paMja.}

\num{4} beTaTxda meVlina saNaNx ububx, duMDu unanxti.

\bentry
\word[no(1)]{no}
\pron{noV}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} (yAvudU) alalxda; ilalxda: \eng{no circumstances
 could justify it} yAvudeV saninxveVshavU adanunx
 samathiRsalAguvudilalx.
\num{2} miVrida; seVrada; oLapaDada; horatAda: \eng{it is no part of
 my plan} adu nananx yoVjanege seVrida saMgatiyalalx. \eng{he is no
 genius} avaneVnU parxtiBA saMpananxnalalx (avanu parxtiBAvaMtara
guMpige seVridavaneVnU alalx).
\num{3} tiVra; tusu; ilalxveV ilalx enunxvaSuTx savxlapx: \eng{he did
 it in no time} avanu adanunx atayxlapx kAladalilx mADida; avanu
adanunx kaSxNAdhaRdalilx mADi mugisida. \eng{it is no distance} adu
dUraveV alalx (adu tiVra hatitxra eMbathaRdalilx).
\num{4} yAvudU sAdhayxvilalx, salalxdu: \eng{there is no accounting

sAdhayxvilalx. \eng{there was no mistaking what he meant} avana
iMgitaveVneMbudanunx tiLiyadiralu sAdhayxveV iralilalx.

parxkaTaNegaLalilx adhAyxhAravAgi: \eng{no parking} (ililx)
vAhanagaLanunx nililxsakUDadu. \eng{no Popery} poVpf adhikAra ililx
salalxdu.}}

\bentry
\word{nominal}
\pron{nAminalf}
\gl{\gu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} nAmavAcakada yA nAmavAcakadaMtha: \eng{nominal roots}
 nAma parxkaqtigaLu.
\num{2} hesarina; hesarinalilxya: \eng{nominal and essential
 distinctions} hesarina matutx vAsatxvika vayxtAyxsagaLu.
\num{3} hesarugaLuLaLx; hesarugaLanunx tiLisuva, namUdisiruva:
\eng{nominal list of officers} adhikArigaLa hesarupaTiTx.
\num{4} hesarige mAtarxviruva; nAmamAtarxda; vAsatxvavalalxda:
\eng{nominal and real rulers} hesarige mAtarx ALuvavaru (`nAmf ke
vAsetx' rAjaru) matutx nijavAgi ALuvavaru.
\num{5} (bADige \mo vugaLa \vi) hesarige mAtarx hAkiruva; atayxlapx
motatxda; nijavAda belegiMta tiVra kaDame iruva: \eng{nominal rent}
hesarige mAtarx hAkiruva (tiVrA kaDame) bADige.
\num{6} hesarugaLuLaLx, hesarugaLanunx tiLisuva, namUdisiruva:
\eng{nominal list of officers} adhikArigaLa hesarupaTiTx.}

\bentry
\word{non-}
\pron{nAnf-}
\gl{\pUparx}
\dictmeaning{niSeVdhAthaRka \pUparx, \kanmu\ 
\num{1} mADada, ilalxda yA saMbaMdhapaDada: \eng{non-attendance} 
 hAjarAgadiruvike; geYru hAjari. \eng{non-payment} pAvati mADadiruvudu.
\num{2} vivarisida vagaRkekx, bagege -- seVrada; \eng{non-alcoholic}
AlakxhAlf vagaRkekx seVrada. \eng{non-member} sadasayxra vagaRkekx seVrada; sadasayxnalalxda.
\num{3} \gu vAgi baLasuva padagaLanunx racisuvalilx: \eng{non-party}
pakaSxkekx seVrirada; pakASxtiVtavAda.
\num{4} ilalxda; aBAvada: \eng{non-access} parxveVsha (mAgaR) ilalxda.
\num{5} (\kirxvi gaLoDane) heVLiruva riVtiyalilx ilalxda:
\eng{non-aggressively} AkarxmaNakAriyAgilalxde.
\num{6} kirxyApadagaLiMda Agada, mADada, udedxVshakakxlalxda eMba
athaRda \gu gaLanunx racisuvalilx: \eng{non-skid} jArada. 
\num{7} \eng{in-} yA \eng{un-} \pUparx gaLiMda racitavAda
niSeVdhAthaRka shabadxgaLu vishiSATxthaRvoMdanonxV
virudAdhxthaRvoMdanonxV koDuva yA visheVSavalalxda sAmAnayx
niSeVdhAthaRvanunx koDuva padagaLanunx racisuvalilx:
\eng{non-effective}
pariNAmakAriyalalxda. \eng{non-human} mAnavanalalxda (Adare
amAnaviVyavAgirada).}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[none(1)]{none}
\pron{nanf}
\gl{\sanA}
{\dictmeaning{oMdU alalx; obabxnU alalx; yAvudU alalx: \eng{none of them
 came} avaralilx obabxnU baralilalx. \eng{none of this concerns
 me} idaralilx yAvudU nanage (savxlapxvU) saMbaMdhisilalx.
\eng{none but fools have ever believed it} mUKaRralalxde (mUKaRranunx
biTuTx) beVre yArU idanunx eMdU naMbilalx.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\eng{none other} beVre yArU alalx, ilalx.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[none(2)]{none}
\pron{nanf}
\gl{\gu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} (pUvoRVkatx \nA kekx saMbaMdhisidaMte) ilalx; EnU
 ilalx: \eng{poetry, we have almost none} kAvayxveMbudu hecucx kaDime
 namamxlilx ilalxveV ilalx. 
\num{2} oMdu nidiRSaTx jAtige, vagaRkekx seVrisalAgada: \eng{if a
 linguist is wanted, I am none} BASA vijAcnxni beVkAgidadxre, nAnaMtU
alalx.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[none(3)]{none}
\pron{nanf}
\gl{\kirxvi}
{\dictmeaning{hececxVnU alalx; savxlapxvU ilalx; ilalxveV ilalx: \eng{I am
 none the wiser for it} adariMda nAneVnU hecucx
 budidhxvaMtanAgalilalx. \eng{the pay is none too high} saMbaLa bahaLa
 jAsitxyeVnU alalx.}}

\num{2} GArxNashakitx; vAsane hiDiyuva shakitx.

\num{6} = \eng{\hyperlink{nosing}{nosing}.}

poliVsarige avara bagegx mAhiti koDuvavanu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1}  \eng{as plain as the nose on your face}
 sapxSaTxvAgide; sapxSaTxvAgi kANisuvaMtide.
\num{2}  \eng{by a nose} atayxlapx aMtaradiMda; savxlapxdaralilx;
\eng{won the race by a nose} atayxlapx aMtaradiMda paMdayxvanunx
gedadx. 
\num{3}  \eng{count noses}

\alnum{a}  hAjariruvavaranunx, beMbala koDuvavaranunx, anumoVdisuvavaranunx lekakx mADu; mUgeNisu.

\alnum{b}  (oMdu viSayavanunx) keVvala saMKAyxbaladiMda nidhaRrisu.
\num{4}  \eng{ get up a (person's) nose} (\ashi) (obabxnanunx) kADu; piVDisu; reVgisu.
\num{5}  \eng{has a good nose} curuku mUgide: 

\alnum{a}  (nAyi \mo vugaLa \vi) vAsane hiDiyuva oLeLx shakitx ide.

\alnum{b}  (\rUpa) (gupatx poliVsaru \mo vara \vi) (aparAdha \mo

ide.

hoLeLxgaLanunx beraLugaLiMda otitxhiDiduko.

vishArxMtiyilalxde, niraMtaravAgi duDi, kelasa mADu.
\num{9}  \eng{\hyperref{kandict_l.pdf}{L}{look(1) nuga(8)}{${}^1$look} down one's nose at}.
\num{10}  \eng{nose of wax} meVNadaMthavanu yA meVNadaMtha vasutx;
sulaBavAgi tidadxbahudAda -- manuSayx, vasutx.
\num{11}  \eng{on the nose}

\alnum{a}  (\ame) (\ashi) sariyAgi; karAruvAkAkxgi.

\alnum{b}  (\AseTxrXV) (\ashi) reVgisuvaMtha; piVDisuvaMtha.

terabeVkAgu.

meVlina munisige mUgu koyudxko; tananx munisiniMda tananx
kelasavanenxV keDisiko;

\bentry
\word{not}
\pron{nATf}
\gl{\kirxvi}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} (\pArxparx) alalx; ilalx: \eng{I know not} nanage gotitxlalx.
\eng{I doubt not} nanage saMshayavilalx.
\num{2} ilalx:

\alnum{a} (sahAyaka \kirx da jate \eng{n't} seVrisidAga) ilalx: \eng{I
can't say} nAnu heVLalAre.
\eng{he'll not come} avanu baruvudilalx. (\ashi) \eng{he ain't here} avanililxlalx.

\alnum{b} (vidhuyxkatx heVLikeyalilx) \eng{did you not tell me} niVnu nanage heVLalilalxveV?
\num{3} kaqdaMtagaLanunx dhAtavxthaRvAcigaLa hiMde niSeVdhAthaR
sUcakavAgi baLasuvAga: \eng{not knowing} tiLiyade. \eng{asked him not
 to come} barabeVDaveMdu avanige heVLide.
\num{4} (niSeVdhAthaRka vAkayx, kirxyApada yA padagucaCxgaLige
adhAyxhAravAgi baruvAga): \eng{``Are you ill?" ``Not at all"} ninage
kAhileyAgideyeV? KaMDita ilalx. \eng{popular or not, it is right}
janapirxyavAgirali biDali, adu sariyAda mAtu hwdu.
\num{5} (payARyavAgi kelavu mAtugaLanunx seVrisutAtx, avugaLalilx
kelavanunx niSeVdhisutAtx mAtanADuvAga) `adu adalalx -- Adare adu
beVroMdu' enunxva hAge: \eng{he is not my son, but yours} avanu nananx
maganalalx, ninanx maga.
\num{6} (oMdu niSeVdhAthaRsUcaka vAkayxda naMtara baruva
savaRnAmavanunx otitx heVLuvAga) \eng{they will not be fooled, not
 they} avaru moVsa hoVgalAraru -- avare? eMdigU ilalx.
\num{7} (\eng{`a'} eMba anideRVshaka guNavAciya hiMde baMdAga, `oMdu
saha ilalx' eMbathaRdalilx) \eng{not a hair of your head shall be
 touched} ninanx taleya oMdu kUdalanunx saha muTuTxvudilalx. 
\num{8} (inonxMdu niSeVdha rUpada shabadxda jate, swmAyxthaR sUcaka
saMdaBaRdalilx baMdAga) \eng{not a few} alapxsavxlapxvalalx (eMdare
`bahaLa' eMbathaRdalilx). \eng{not seldom} aparUpavAgalalx;
omomxmemxyalalx (eMdare `aneVka veVLe' eMbathaRdalilx).}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{as likely as not} eSuTx saMBavavoV aSeTxV
asaMBavavU hwdu.
\num{2} \eng {not at all} (yArAdarU kaqtajacnxte sUcisidAga
shiSATxcArakAkxgi utatxra koDutAtx) aMthadeVnU ilalx; hAge niVvu
heVLuva agatayxvilalx.
\num{3} \eng{not a thing} yAvudU ilalx oMdU ilalx.
\num{4} \eng{not but that}= \hyperlink{notpagu16}{\pagu\ ($16$)}.
\num{5} \eng{not but}(\pArxparx) = \hyperlink{notpagu16}{\pagu\ ($16$)}.
\num{6} \eng{no \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{half(3) nuga}{${}^3$half}}.
\num{7} \eng{not least} kaDame pArxmuKayxvalalx (eMdare sAkaSuTx parxmuKavAda).
\num{8} \eng{not \hyperref{kandict_m.pdf}{M}{much(3) pagu(6)}{${}^3$much}}.
\num{9} \eng{not once nor twice}= \hyperlink{notpagu10}{\pagu\ ($10$)}.
\hypertarget{notpagu10}{}
\num{10} \eng{not once or twice} oMderaDu salavalalx; aneVka bAri.
\num{11} \eng{not quite}:

\alnum{a} hecucx kaDame.

\alnum{b} aSeTxVnU alalx; bhuteVka:
\eng{it is not quite proper} adu aSeTxVnU ucitavalalx. 
\hypertarget{notpagu12}{}
\num{12} \eng{not so well} aSeTxVnU oLeLxyadalalxda (riVtiyalilx).
\hyperdef{N}{not pagu(13)}{}
\num{13} \eng{not that} hAgeMdu athaRvalalx, Adare: \eng{if he said
 so-not that he ever did-he lied} avanu hAge heVLidadxre -- hAge
eMdigU heVLiralAra -- adu suLuLx.
\num{14} \eng{not too well} = \hyperlink{notpagu12}{\pagu\ ($12$)}.
\num{15} \eng{not \hyperref{kandict_v.pdf}{V}{very(2) pagu(1)}{${}^2$very}}.
\hypertarget{notpagu16}{}
\num{16} \eng{not but what}(\pArxparx)

\alnum{a} adeVneV irali; AdarU; hAgidadxrU: \eng{ not what I can do it,
 not but that a stronger man might} nAnu adanunx mADalAre; adeVneV
irali nanagiMta shakatxnAdavanu adanunx mADirutitxdadx.

\alnum{b} aMthadadxlalx; aMthavanalalx: \eng{not such a fool but what he
 can see it}adanunx kANadiruvaSuTx avanu daDaDxnalalx.}

\bentry
\word[nothing(1)]{nothing}
\pron{natiMgf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (guNavAcakada hiMde baMdAga) yAvudeV vasutx alalx, ilalx(dudx):
\eng{nothing great is easy} mahatavxvAdadudx yAvudU sulaBavalalx. \eng{nothing has been done}
EnanUnx mADalAgilalx; yAvudU Agilalx. \eng{have nothing to do} mADalu (kelasa) EnU ilalx.
\num{2} (kelamomemx pUrakavAkayxda joteylilx) yAvudU, EnU ilalx: \eng{I see nothing that I want}
nanage beVkAda yAvudU nanage kANutitxlalx. \eng{can find nothing
useful} upayukatxvAda yAvudU
ilalx.
\num{3} 
\alnum{a} kuSxlalxkavAda -- vasutx, saMgati, mAtu yA vayxkitx: \eng{was nothing to me}
adu nanage kuSxlalxkavAda viSayavAgitutx. \eng{the little nothings of
life} jiVvanada kuSxlalxka
viSayagaLu. \eng{he is nothing without his money} avana baLi haNavilalxde hoVgidadxre
avanobabx kelasakekx bArada vayxkitx.

\alnum{b} (visheVSaNavAgi, \AmA) agaNayx; beleyilalxda: \eng{a nothing sort of day}
oMdu riVti agaNayxvAda dina.
\num{4} aBAva; ilalxme; ilalxdiruvike; ilalxdiruvudu; nAsitx.
\num{5} (aMkagaNita, lekAkxcAradalilx) sonenx -- aMka, mobalagu,
itAyxdi: \eng{multiply 6 by nothing, and the result is nothing}
Aranunx sonenxyiMda guNisidare sonenx barutatxde. \eng{a third of
 nothing is nothing} sonenxya mUraneV oMdu BAga sonenxyeV.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{be nothing}(dhamaRda \vi)

\alnum{a} yAva nidiRSaTx paMgaDakUkx seVradiru.

\alnum{b} nAsitxkanAgiru.

\alnum{c} ajecnxVyatAvAdiyAgiru.
\num{2} \eng{be nothing to}

\alnum{a} saMbaMdha beVDadiru; saMbaMdhisiradiru: \eng{it is nothing
to do with me} adakUkx
nanagU saMbaMdhavilalx.

\alnum{b} hoVlikeyAgadiru; hoVlike ilalxdiru.
\num{3} \eng{be (\engit{or} have) nothing to do with}

\alnum{a} (vasutx yA vayxkitxya \vi) saMbaMdha ilalxdiru; goDave ilalxdiru; usAbari beVDadiru.

\alnum{b} (yAvudeV oMdaralilx yA oMdaroDane) saMbaMdha hoMdadiru, seVradiru.
\num{4} \eng{come to nothing} niSaPxlavAgu; vayxthaRvAgi pariNamisu; EnU parxyoVjanavAgadiru:
\eng{hopes that come to nothing} vayxthaRvAgi pariNamisuva BaravasegaLu; niSapxla
niriVkeSxgaLu.
\num{5} \eng{count (\engit{or} go) for nothing} gaNanege bAradiru; vayxthaRvAgu.
\num{6} \eng{feel like nothing on earth}(\AmA) tiVvarxvAda asavxsathxte yA mujugara
anuBavisu.
\num{7} \eng{for nothing}

\alnum{a} pukakxTeyAgi.

\alnum{b} vayxthaRvAgi; EnU parxyoVjanavilalxde.
\num{8} \eng{has nothing in him} avanobabx nagaNayx; yaHkashicxtf manuSayx; avanige yAva 
vayxkitxtavxvU ilalx.
\hyperdef{N}{nothing(1) pagu(9)}{}
\num{9} \eng{have nothing on}

\alnum{a} (yAvudoV oMdakikxMta) hecucx anukUla hoMdilalxdiru.

\alnum{b} (obabxna bagegx) AkeSxVpaNiVyavAda EnanUnx hoMdadiru, gotitxlalxdiru. 

\alnum{c} (vayxMgayx) (yAvudoV oMdakikxMta) tiVrA kiVLAgiru.

\alnum{d} bari meYyalilxru; betatxleyAgiru.

\alnum{e} biDuvAgiru; yAvudeV kelasakAyRgaLilalxdiru.
\num{10} \eng{is nothing to}

\alnum{a} EnU lekakxvilalx; yAvudakUkx ilalx; taqNasamAna: \eng{money is nothing to him}
haNa eMdare avanige taqNasamAna.

\alnum{b} (adara) samAnakekx baralAradu; (adakUkx, idakUkx) hoVlike ilalx.
\num{11} \eng{like nothing on earth}(\AmA) (kurUpa \mo vugaLa \vi) atayxMta; vipariVtavAda;
ati hecicxna: \eng{look like nothing on earth}(\AmA):

\alnum{a} tiVrA avalakaSxNavAgiru; bahaLa kurUpiyAgiru.

\alnum{b} ati ADaMbaradiMda tuMbiru; kaNiNxge rAcuvaMtiru.

\num{12} \eng{make nothing of}

\alnum{a} laGuvAgeNisu; alapxveMdu BAvisu.

\alnum{b} hiMjariyade -- mADu, naDesu.

\alnum{c} EnU mADalu toVcadiru, athaRvAgadiru.

\alnum{d} upayoVgisalu, baLasalu sAdhayxvilalxvAgu.

\alnum{e} vayxvaharisalu sAdhayxvilalxvAgu.
\num{13} \eng{mean nothing to}

\alnum{a} athaRvilalxvAgu.

\alnum{b} mecacxdaMtAgu.

\alnum{c} AshisadaMtAgu.
\num{14} \eng{neck or nothing} AdadAdxgaleMdu; savaRsavxvanUnx paNavAgi oDiDx.
\num{15} \eng{no nothing}(\AmA) (ilalxda padAthaRgaLa paTiTxyalilx heVLuva koneya mAtu)
yAvudU ilalx; oMdU ilalx: \eng{no bread, no butter, no cheese, no nothing}berxDf ilalx,
beNeNx ilalx, ciVsf\kern -1ptZ ilalx, yAvudU ilalx.
\num{16} \eng{nothing but} = \hyperlink{nothingpagu18}{\pagu\ $(18)$}.
\num{17} \eng{nothing doing}

\alnum{a} (\AmA) muKayxvAdadudx EnU sAdhayxvAgadu; gamanAhaRvAdudeVnU Agutitxlalx:
\eng{there was nothing doing in town} Urinalilx gamanAhaRvAdudeVnU naDeyutitxlalx.

\alnum{b} KaMDita ilalx; eMdeMdigU sAdhayxvilalx.
\hypertarget{nothingpagu18}{}
\num{18} \eng{nothing else but (\engit{or} than)} sumamxne; keVvala; baride; nisasxMdeVhavAgi;
nisasxMshayavAgi: \eng{did nothing but grumble} goNaguvudanunx biTuTx EnanUnx mADalilalx;
sumamxne (goNagida).
\num{19} \eng{nothing for it but to} vidhiyilalx; upAyavilalx; adanunx biTuTx beVre
mAgaRvilalx.
\num{20} \eng{nothing if not} muKayxvAgi; mUlataH: \eng{it is nothing if not critical}
 tapupx kaMDuhiDiyuvudu biTuTx beVreVnU alalx; tapupx kaMDu hiDiyuvudoMdeV muKayx lakaSxNa.
\num{21} \eng{nothing less than}

\alnum{a} kaDime Enalalx: \eng{expected nothing less than a riot} kaDeV pakaSx doMbi
AgutatxdeMdeV niriVkiSxsida; doMbiyAdarU AgiyeV tiVrutatxdeMdu niriVkiSxsida.

\alnum{b} (\viparx) idakekx tiVrA virudadhxvAda.

\alnum{c} (\viparx) eMdeMdigU ilalx; savxlapxvU ilalx.
\num{22} \eng{nothing like leather} tananx saraku elalx kelasakUkx odagutatxde (eMba
sAvxBimAnada aBipArxya).
\num{23} \eng{nothing venture nothing have}(gelalxbeVkAdare mununxgagxbeVku eMbathaRdalilx)
dheYyaRvU ilalx, lABavU ilalx.
\num{24} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{stop(1) pagu(4)}{${}^1$stop} at nothing.}
\num{25} \eng{there is nothing in it}

\alnum{a} adu nijavalalx.

\alnum{b} adeVnU muKayxvalalx.

\alnum{c} adaralilx EnU toDakilalx.

\alnum{d} (ibabxra peYki) yArigU adaralilx hecicxna parxyoVjana yA anukUla ilalx.
\num{26} \eng{there is nothing to it} adu nijavalalx; adeVnU muKayxvalalx; adu tiVrA saraLa,
neVra.
\num{27} \eng{think nothing of it}(kaSxme keVLabeVDa yA kaqtajacnxte toVrisabeVkeMba
BAvaneyiTuTxkoLaLxbeVDa eMdu sUcisalu baLasuva mAtAgi) adanunx yoVcisabeVDa; hAge ciMtisabeVDa.
\num{28} \eng{to nothing} karxmeVNa saMpUNaRvAgi -- horaTuhoVgi, kANadAgi, adaqshayxvAgi.
\num{29} \eng{to say nothing (of)}(aSuTx muKayxvalalxda aMshavanunx heVLuvAga yA muKayx
aMshavanunx AlaMkArikavAgi heVLuvAga) (adanunx) heVLabeVkAdudilalx.
\num{30} \eng{with nothing on}

\alnum{a} betatxleyAgi; barimeYyalilx.

\alnum{b} sAkaSuTx (meYmucucxvaSuTx) baTeTx hAkikoLaLxde.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[now(1)]{now}
\pron{nw}
\gl{\kirxvi}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} Iga; sadayxdalilx; I hotitxnalilx; I hotitxge.
\num{2} I -- kaSxNa, kUDaleV; tatfkaSxNa: \eng{I must go home now} I kaSxNa nAnu manege
hoVgabeVku.
\num{3} ukatx kAladalilx; heVLida -- hotitxnalilx, samayadalilx.
\num{4} I yA A -- hotitxge, kAlakekx \eng{! it was now clear} A hotitxge adu sapxSaTxvAgitutx.
\num{5} Iga; parxkaqta saMdaBaRdalilx: \eng{I cannot now agree} parxkaqta saMdaBaRdalilx
nAnu opapxlu sAdhayxvilalx.
\num{6} I muMdina saninxveVshadalilx, parisithxtiyalilx: \eng{I cannot now ever believe you
again} inunx eMdigU nAnu ninanxnunx naMbalAre.
\num{7} I hiMde; savxlapx hiMde; Iga tAne: \eng{just now} Iga tAne; savxlapx hotitxna hiMde.
\num{8} (\kanmu\ kathanadalilx yA saMBASaNeyalilx) Aga; taruvAya; AmeVle; naMtara; anaMtara:
\eng{Caeser now marched east} Aga siVsa\kern 1ptZrf pUvaR dikikxna kaDe muMduvarida.
\eng{now let us consider the second point} AmeVle eraDaneV viSayavanunx parishiVlisoVNa.
\num{9} (kAlavanunx sUcisade AkeSxVpaNe, beVDike, bedarike, vivaraNe, samajAyiSi, \mo\
saMdaBaRgaLalilx takakxMte dhavxnikoTuTx \parx) ililx keVLi; nAnu -- beVDuteVtxne,
otAtxyisutetxVne, ecacxrike koDutitxdedxVne; AdarU idanunx tiLidirabeVku; idanunx
opipxkoLaLxbeVku; KaMDitavAgi (eMba athaRgaLalilx \parx): \eng{now what do you mean by it?}
hAgeMdare, Enu aMta niVnu heVLoVdu? \eng{now then don`t cry} hoVgali aLabeVDa, sumamxniru.
\eng{now, now behave yourself!} noVDu, noVDu, Iga sariyAgi naDeduko!
\num{10} inunx -- meVle, muMde: \eng{well what do you want now?} sari, inunx muMde
ninageVnAgabeVku?}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{but now} = \hyperlink{nowpagu2}{\pagu $(2)$}.
\hypertarget{nowpagu2}{}
\num{2} \eng{even now} IgaSeTxV.
\num{3} \eng{every now and again} = \hyperlink{nowpagu5}{\pagu $(5)$}.
\num{4} \eng{how now?}(\pArxparx) Enu viSaya? idarathaRveVnu?
\hypertarget{nowpagu5}{}
\num{5} \eng{now and then} AgAga; matetx matetx; padeV padeV; punaH punaH.
\num{6} \eng{now for it!} idiVga takakx samaya.
\hyperdef{N}{now(1) pagu(7)}{}
\num{7} \eng{now or never} Iga biTaTxre hoVyitu.}
\eentry

 with cold} caLiyiMda maragaTiTxda.}

\bentry
\word[number(1)]{number}
\pron{naMbarf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} aMki; saMKeyx: \eng{six is an even number} Aru eMbudu samasaMKeyx.
\num{2} aMki; saMKeyx:

\alnum{a} aMkiyanunx sUcisuva shabadx, saMkeVta yA citarx.

\alnum{b} gurutu, parAmashaRne, \mo vugaLigAgi, oMdu gotAtxda motatxda
sherxVNiyalilx yAvudAdarU oMdanunx nideRVshisuvAga adakekx [\udA\
vAhanagaLu, dUravANi, \mo vakekx] koDuva saMKeyx, aMki:
\eng{registration number} noVMdaNi saMKeyx. 
\num{3} (janara, vasutxgaLa oTuTx motatx sUcisuva) aMki; saMKeyx: \eng{what number of people are
you expecting?} niVnu oTuTx eSuTx saMKeyxya janaranunx niriVkiSxsutitxdidxVye? \eng{the number
of accidents has decreased} apaGAtagaLa saMKeyx kaDameyAgide. \eng{twenty in number}
(saMKeyxyalilx) ipapxtitxve.
\num{4} (\bava dalilx) gaNita; aMkagaNita: \eng{not good at numbers} gaNitadalilx kushalanalalx.
\num{5} (\Eva\ yA \bava dalilx) parxmANa; motatx: \eng{a large number
of people} BAri motatxda
janaru. \eng{only in small numbers} kaDame parxmANadalilx mAtarx.
\num{6} aMki; saMKeyx; oMdu sherxVNiyalilx iMtiSaTxneyadu eMdu sUcisuva cihenx (\kanmu\ vaqtatx
patirxkeya iMtha saMcike, giVtanATakadalilx yA saMgiVta kaceVriyalilx iMtiSaTxneya hADu, \mo vu).
\num{7} jate; jote; guMpu; vagaR: \eng{he is of our number} avanu namamx guMpinavanu. \eng{among
our number} namamx guMpinalilx.
\num{8} (\vAyx) vacana: \eng{Sanskrit has three numbers} saMsakxqqta BASeyalilx mUru vacanagaLive.
\num{9} (\AmA) (saligeyiMda yA pirxVtiyiMda vayxkitxyanunx yA vasutxvanunx kareyuvAga) naMbaru;
isamu: \eng{an attractive little number} AkaSaRkavAda puTaTx vayxkitx, vasutx.
\num{10} \eng{(Numbers)}(\beY) saMKAyxkAMDa; haLeya oDaMbaDikeyalilx janagaNatiyiruva
nAlakxneya adhAyxya.
\num{11} oMdu gotAtxda saMKeyxyavaregiruvudaralilx nidiRSaTxvAgi yAvudAdarU oMdu vasutx,
vayxkitx, \mo vu: \eng{number 22 wants his boots} ipapxtetxraDaneya isamu, vayxkitx bUTugaLu
beVkenunxtAtxne.
\num{12} (\AmA) vayxkitx, uDupu, kelasa, \mo vu.
\num{13} (\bava dalilx) saMKAyxbala; saMKeyxya hecacxLa: \eng{they won by force of numbers}
avaru keVvala saMKAyxbaladiMda gedadxru.
\num{14} eNike.
\num{15} (\pArxparx) tALa; laya.
\num{16} (\bava dalilx)

\alnum{a} (\saM) savxrataMDa.

\alnum{b} (\CaM) gaNagaLu.

\alnum{c} (padayxda) sAlugaLu; caraNagaLu; paMkitxgaLu.

\alnum{d} padayxgaLu; kAvayx: \eng{I lisped in numbers for the numbers
came} nAnu todalu
mAtanADutitxruvaMteyeV kAvayx raciside; yAkeMdare kAvayx nananxlilx
tAneV tAnAgi suPxrisitu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{a number of}

\alnum{a} kelavu.

\alnum{b} halvAru; aneVka (\bava da kirxyApadadoDane baLake Iga sAmAnayx): \eng{a number of
problems remain} halavAru samaseyxgaLu hAgeyeV uLidive.
\num{2} \eng{by numbers} saMKAyxnusAra; saMKeyxgaLiMda sUcitavAda saraLa nideRVshagaLanunx
anusarisi.
\num{3} \eng{have a person's number}(\ashi) obabxna nijavAda savxBAva, udedxVsha, \mo vanunx
tiLiduko, athaRmADiko.
\num{4} \eng{have a person's number on it}(bAMbf guMDu, \mo vugaLa \vi) nidiRSaTx
vayxkitxyanunx hoDeyuvaMte niyatavAgiru.
\num{5} \eng{in number} eNikeyalilx; eNisidalilx; saMKeyxyalilx: \eng{one people exceeds another
in number} oMdu janAMga inonxMdanunx saMKeyxyalilx mIrisutatxde.
\num{6} \eng{in numbers}(kathe \mo\ parxkaTaNegaLa \vi) anukarxmavAgi baruva saMcikegaLalilx;
saMKAyxnukarxmada BAgagaLalilx.
\num{7} \eng{in small number} kaDime saMKeyxyalilx; viraLa parxmANadalilx.
\num{8} \eng{make one's number with}(\ashi) (obabxna jote) saMpakaR hoMdu; obabxnanunx
BeVTiyAgu, kANu, saMpakiRsu.
\num{9} \eng{numbers game} (\hiV) keVvala aMkagaNitada (lekAkxcAra)vanonxLagoMDa kelasa.
\num{10} \eng{Number Ten} hatutx; DwniMgf siTxrXVTf; iMgelxMDina parxdhAniya adhikaqta laMDanf
nivAsa.
\num{11} \eng{number two} eraDaneya sAthxnadalilxruva; divxtiVya sAthxnada.
\num{12} \eng{one's number is up}(\AmA) avanu sAyutAtxne; avana kathe mugiyutatxde.
\num{13} \eng{out of number} = \hyperlink{numberpagu16}{\pagu $(16)$}.
\num{14} \eng{round numbers} (cilalxre saMKeyx biTuTx baruva) pUNARMkagaLu; pUNaR saMKeyxgaLu
(\udA\ \eng{10, 20, 100,} \mo vu).
\num{15} \eng{to the number of}(yAvudoV) aMkiyavarege; saMKeyxyavarege: \eng{to the number of
80} eMbatatxravarege.
\hypertarget{numberpagu16}{}
\num{16} \eng{without number} asaMKAyxta; agaNita; lekakxvilalxdaSuTx.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[number(2)]{number}
\pron{naMbarf}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} (oMdu vagaRdalilx) seVrisu; seVridedxMdu eNisu: \eng{I number you among my
friends} nAnu ninanxnunx nananx senxVhitaralilx seVrisidedxVne, niVnu seVrididxVyeMdu
eNisutetxVne.
\num{2} (yAvudakAkxdarU) oMdu saMKeyx yA saMKeyxgaLanunx koDu; oMdu saMKeyxyiMda nideRVshisu.
\num{3} (oMdu nidiRSaTx saMKeyxyaSuTx) motatxvAgu; (aSuTx) saMKeyxyalilxru: \eng{the crew and
passengers numbered thirty-three} haDaginalilx sibabxMdi parxyANikaru seVri mUvatatxmUru maMdi
idadxru.
\num{4} eNisu; lekakx mADu; saMKeyxyanunx gotutxmADu.
\num{5} oLagoLuLx; oLagoMDiru.
\num{6} (\kaparx dalilx) saMKeyxyalilx -- parimitavAgiru, siVmitagoLuLx.
\num{7} (iSuTx vaSaR) tuMbiru; badukiru; jiVvisu: \eng{of as able body as when he numbered
thirty} avanu mUvatutx vaSaRdavanAgidAdxga idadxMte daqDhakAya.
\num{8} (iMtiSuTx saMKeyxya nivAsigaLu, vasutxgaLu, \mo vugaLiMda) kUDiru; tuMbiru: \eng{Mysore
numbers eight lakh inhabitants} meYsUru eMTu lakaSx nivAsigaLiMda
tuMbide.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\eng{one's days are numbered}(obabxna) dinagaLu mugiyutatx
 baMdavu; hecucx dina badukuvudilalx.}
\eentry

\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} dAdi; Aya; roVgigaLa, ashakatxra upacAradalilx veYdayxrige neravAguva, tarabeVtu paDediruva vayxkitx.
\num{2} dhAtirx makakxLa dAdi; cikakx makakxLa yoVgakeSxVma mAtarx noVDikoLuLxva dAdi.
\num{3} (\pArxparx) satxnayx dAdi; moleyUDuva dAdi; beVreyavara
maguvige moleyUDisi AreYke mADalu neVmitaLAda heMgasu \eng{(=
\hyperref{kandict_w.pdf}{W}{wet-nurse(1)}{wetnurse}).}
\num{4} (araNayx vijAcnxna) poVSaka, Asharxya -- vaqkaSx; itara sasayxgaLige Asharxya niVDuvudakAkxgiyeV beLesida mara.
\num{5} (\pArxvi) poVSaka kiVTa; kelasagAra kiVTa; kiVTada marigaLanunx poVSisuva, leYMgika doVSaviruva jeVnunoNa, kiVTa, itAyxdi.
\num{6} poVSaka; oMdu vishiSaTx guNa \mo vanunx beLesuva deVsha \mo
vu: \eng{ the nurd of liberty} sApxtaMtarxyxda poVSaka.
\num{7} poVSaNe; AreYke.
\num{8} moleyUDuvudu yA moleyUDisalapxDuvudu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{at nurd} dAdiya poVSaNeyalilx, AreYkeyalilx.
\num{2} \eng{put out to nurd} 

\alnum{a} (maguvina \vi) dAdiya vashakekx koDu; dAdiya poVSaNege,
AreYkege -- opipxsu.

\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (Asitx \mo vugaLa \vi) Asitxyanunx pAlisuvavara vashakekx opipxsu, koDu. }

\bentry
\word[nurse(2)]{nurse}
\pron{nasfR}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (roVgige) shushUrxSe, AreYke -- mADu.
\num{2} (kAyile, gAyavAda deVhada aMga, \mo vanunx) vAsimADikoLaLxlu yatinxsu.
\num{3} (maguvige) moleyuNisu; satxnayx koDu; moleyUDisuva dAdiyAgiru.
\num{4} (\kaparx dalilx) (oMdu nidiRSaTx sithxtiyalilx) beLasalAgiru:
\eng{nursed in pomp and pleasure} suKasaMpatitxnalilx
beLasida. \eng{nursed in poverty} baDatanadalilx beLasida.
\num{5} (ecacxrikeyiMda yA pirxVtiyiMda) hiDiduko yA apipxkoMDu
mudAdxDu: \eng{sat nursing my feet} nananx kAlugaLanunx apipxkoMDu
kuLita(Lu).
\num{6} (sasayxgaLu, kalegaLu, \mo vanunx) beLasu; poVSisu; aBivadhiRsu; aBivaqdidhxpaDisu.
\num{7} (koragu, devxVSa, \mo vanunx) beLasu; poVSisu: \eng{to nurse a
 grudge} manasisxnalilx jididxTuTxko.
\num{8} ecacxrikeyiMda noVDiko; gamanaviTuTx noVDiko; visheVSa gamana
koDu: \eng{nurse the voters} matakeSxVtarxda vishAvxsavanunx
hiDidiTuTxko; matadAraranunx sadA OleYsutAtx, upacarisutAtx
(tananxlilx) vishAvxsavuLaLxvaranAnxgi mADiko, iTuTxko. \eng{ to nurse
 the borough cost him Rs. 50,000/- a year} tananx keSxVtarxda
matadAraranunx vishAvxsadalilxTuTxkoLaLxlu avanige parxtivaSaR
\eng{50,000/-} rUpAyigaLa KacuR tagulitu.
\num{9} (bilayxDf\char 144R) ATagArana ceMDiniMda oMdAda meVloMdu ceMDu
hoDeyalAguvaMte (ceMDugaLanunx) karxmadalilx seVrisi iTiTxru.}}

\bentry
\word[nut(1)]{nut}
\pron{naTf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} 
\alnum{a} karaTakAyi; gaDusAda yA metuvAda cipipxnoLagaDe AhArayoVgayx tiruLiruva kAyi, haNuNx.

\alnum{b} I karaTa.
\num{2} gaTiTx biVjaviruva biVjakoVsha.
\num{3} naTuTx; boVlaTxnunx hAki tirugisuvaMte, raMdharxdalilx tirupu
gADigaLuLaLx, \sA\ cacwcxka yA SaDuBxjAkArada tirupu.
\num{4} (\ashi) tale; talekAyi ; taleburuDe.
\num{5} (\ashi)

\alnum{a} hucacx; tikakxla(manuSayx).

\alnum{b} Bakatx; kaTATx aBimAni: perxVmi: \eng{an exercise nut} vAyxyAmada Bakatx, kaTATxBimAni.
\num{6} (kalilxdadxlu, beNeNx, \mo vugaLa) uMDe; mudedx; tuNuku; saNaNx tuMDu.
\num{7} 
\alnum{a} piTiVlu kamAnu \mo vugaLalilxna kudureya javi \mo
vanunx bigisuva yA saDilisuva biraDe, hiDike.

\alnum{b} (piTiVlu \mo\ taMtivAdayxgaLalilxna) kudure; taMtigaLu
hAyuvaMte vAdayxda kaMThada tudiyalilx neleyAgi nililxsiruva kudure.
\num{8} (\bava dalilx) (ashilxVla \ashi) taraDu; taraDu biVja. 
\num{9} (\pArxparx) (\ashi) SoVkiVlAla; sogasugAra puTaTxsAmi.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{do one's nut}(\ashi) atiyAgi koVpagoMDiru, siDimiDigoMDiru.
\num{2} \eng{for nuts} (\ashi) sumArAgi kUDa; alapxsavxlapx cenAnxgi
saha: \eng{can't shoot for nuts} savxlapx cenAnxgi kUDa hoDeyalAra.
\num{3} \eng{nuts and bolts}(\rUpa) oMdu kelasada vAyxvahArika vivaragaLu.
\num{4} \eng{off one's nut} tale keTiTxru; hucucx hiDidiru.}

\bentry
\word{nut-oil}
\pron{naTfAilf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{kAyeNeNx; naTf eNeNx; heVsaZlfkAyi, vAlanxTf, akorxVTf, \mo\
 cipupxkAyigaLiMda tegeda, raMgugaLu matutx vAniRSfgaLalilx baLasuva,
 oMdu bageya eNeNx.}
\eentry

 vaMshakekx seVrida, KAdayxPala koDuva, tALeyaMtha mara.}

 biVjagaLiruva, \kanu\ amerikada peYnf mara.}

\alnum{b} AhAra; poVSaka vasutx.
\num{2} poVSaNa shAsatxrX; poVSaNeya shAsitxrXVya adhayxyana.}

\bentry
\word[nuts(1)]{nuts}
\pron{naTfsx}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{(\ashi) hucucxhiDida; tikakxlu hiDida.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\eng{nuts about (\engit{or} on)}(\AmA) (oMdu viSayadalilx)

\alnum{a} utAsxhiyAda; utusxkanAgiruva.

\alnum{b} catura; kushala.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[nuts(2)]{nuts}
\pron{naTfsx}
\gl{\BAavayx}
\dictmeaning{(\ashi) (tirasAkxra yA aNaka sUcisuva udAgxra) thU; thu:
\eng{ nuts to you} thU ninanx!}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{nutshell}
\pron{naTfSelf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} kAyi -- karaTa, cipupx.
\num{2} (\rUpa) (heVLuvudaralilx) atayxMta saMgarxha rUpa; saMkiSxpatx
nirUpaNe; bahaLa aDaka riVti: \eng{can give it to you in a nutshell} ninagadanunx aDakavAgi heVLabalelx.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{nutty}
\pron{naTi}
\gl{\gu}(\tara\ \eng{nuttier}, \tama\ \eng{nuttiest}).
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} 
\alnum{a} karaTakAyi -- tuMbida, Barita; heVraLavAgi karaTakAyi biDuva.

\alnum{b} karaTakAyi ruciya.
\num{2} (\ashi) = \eng{\hyperlink{nuts(1)}{${}^1$nuts}.}}

\bentry

\pron{nakfsxvAmika}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} kAjavAra; hemumxSiTx; viSamuSiTx; siTxrXkAnxsfnakfsx
 vAmika kulakekx seVrida, viSa haNuNxgaLanunx biDuva, pUvaR iMDiyAda
 mara.
\num{2} siTxrXkinxVnf eMba AlakxlAyfDx iruva I marada biVjagaLu.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{nuzzle}
\pron{nasa\kern 1ptZ(sf\kern -1ptZ)lf}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} melalxge mUginiMda ujujx, tivi.
\num{2} (\AtAmx\ saha) becacxge -- oLage tUriko, mudurikoMDiru.}}

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} mUginiMda -- otutx, ujujx; mUganunx(oMdaroLakekx) nUku.
\num{2} mUginiMda mUsi noVDu.
\num{3} mUginiMda bila toVDu.}

\bentry
\word{nylon}
\pron{neYlAnf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} neYlAnf; keYgArikegaLalilx, baTeTxgaLalilx, hagagx
 tayArikeyalilx, inUnx vividha keSxVtarxgaLalilx baLasutitxruva,
 daqDhavU haguravU ilAsiTxkf guNagaLanUnx uLaLx, porxVTiVninaMtha
 racaneyuLaLx halavAru saMshelxVSita kaqtaka pAli ameYDfgaLalilx
 oMdu.
\num{2} neYlAnf baTeTx.
\num{3} (\bava dalilx) neYlAnf(niMda tayArisida) kAluciVlagaLu.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{nymph}
\pron{niMphf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{\num{1} apasxre; (kaDalu, hoLe, kAraMji, beTaTx, kADu, mara
 \mo vugaLalilx nelesiruva, yA meVlatxrada deVvategaLige
 parivAravAgiruva) purANada sitxrXV upadeVvate(gaLalolxbabxLu).
\num{2} (\kAparx) apasxre; suMdari; suMdara taruNi.
\num{3} niMphf; vayasakx kiVTavanunx hoVluva, pArxyakekx baMdilalxda kiVTa.
\num{4} cikakx koDati huLu yA tUkada huLu.}
\eentry
